</div>
				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Egg cycles</h1>

				<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
					<div id="siteSub">From Bulbapedia, the community-driven Pokémon encyclopedia.</div>
					<div id="contentSub"></div>
										<div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump">Jump to: <a href="#column-one">navigation</a>, <a href="#searchInput">search</a></div>

					<!-- start content -->
					<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><table style="background: #FAFFF4; border: 2px solid #F85888; width: 75%; border-radius: 30px; -moz-border-radius: 30px; -webkit-border-radius: 30px; -khtml-border-radius: 30px; -icab-border-radius: 30px; -o-border-radius: 30px;; margin: auto">

<tr>
<td style="background:#FA92B2; padding: 10px; width: 80px; border-radius: 50px; -moz-border-radius: 50px; -webkit-border-radius: 50px; -khtml-border-radius: 50px; -icab-border-radius: 50px; -o-border-radius: 50px;; text-align:right"> <a href="/wiki/File:201Unown.png" class="image" title="Get it? </td>

</td></tr></table>

<tr>
<td style="background:#C6B7F5; padding: 10px; text-align:center; border-radius: 50px; -moz-border-radius: 50px; -webkit-border-radius: 50px; -khtml-border-radius: 50px; -icab-border-radius: 50px; -o-border-radius: 50px;" width="50px"> <a href="/wiki/File:018Pidgeot.png" class="image"><img alt="018Pidgeot.png" src="http://cdn.bulbagarden.net/upload/thumb/5/57/018Pidgeot.png/50px-018Pidgeot.png" width="50" height="50" srcset="http://cdn.bulbagarden.net/upload/thumb/5/57/018Pidgeot.png/75px-018Pidgeot.png 1.5x, http://cdn.bulbagarden.net/upload/thumb/5/57/018Pidgeot.png/100px-018Pidgeot.png 2x" /></a>
</td>
<td> <b>It has been suggested that this article be moved to <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/w/index.php?title=Egg_cycle&amp;action=edit"><span style="color:#CC2200"><span title="Egg cycle">Egg cycle</span></a></span>.</b><br />Please discuss whether or not to move it on its <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Talk:Egg_cycles">talk page</a></span>.
</td></tr></table>
<hr />
<p>An <b>Egg cycle</b> is a unit of time measured in steps that determines how long it will take for a <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Egg" title="Pokémon Egg">Pokémon Egg</a> to hatch. The number of Egg cycles required to hatch an Egg is stored in the same number that would be the <a href="/wiki/Friendship" title="Friendship">friendship</a> value for normal Pokémon. In all games since <a href="/wiki/Generation_V" title="Generation V">Generation V</a>, the length of an Egg cycle is 257 steps. In <a href="/wiki/Generation_IV" title="Generation IV">Generation IV</a>, Egg cycles were 255 steps long, while in Generations <a href="/wiki/Generation_II" title="Generation II">II</a> and <a href="/wiki/Generation_III" title="Generation III">III</a>, they were 256 steps long.
</p>
<div id="toc" class="toc"><div id="toctitle"><h2>Contents</h2></div>

</ul>
</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Generation_V_and_later">Generation V and later</span></h2>
<p>Every time an Egg cycle is completed, the Egg cycle count for all Eggs in the player's <a href="/wiki/Party" title="Party">party</a> is decreased by 1 (by 2 if a Pokémon with <a href="/wiki/Flame_Body_(Ability)" title="Flame Body (Ability)">Flame Body</a> or <a href="/wiki/Magma_Armor_(Ability)" title="Magma Armor (Ability)">Magma Armor</a> is also in the party, but not below 0). An Egg is ready to hatch as soon as its Egg cycle count reaches 0. If multiple Eggs are ready to hatch after an Egg cycle ends, the first Egg in the party will hatch immediately, while the remaining Eggs will hatch&#8212;in order and one at a time&#8212;each time the player takes another step.
</p><p>Using a Hatching Power (from <a href="/wiki/Entralink#Pass_Powers" title="Entralink">Pass Powers</a> or <a href="/wiki/O-Power" title="O-Power">O-Powers</a>) will shorten the length of an Egg cycle depending on the strength of the Power used.
</p>
<ul><li> Weak: <sup>4</sup>/<sub>5</sub> (205 steps)</li>
<li> Medium: <sup>2</sup>/<sub>3</sub> (171 steps)</li>
<li> Strong: <sup>1</sup>/<sub>2</sub> (129 steps)</li></ul>
<p>The number of steps walked in the current Egg cycle is also modified by the appropriate multiplier above. When the Hatching Power wears off, the current number of steps walked in the current Egg cycle is divided by the same multiplier.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Omega_Ruby_and_Alpha_Sapphire" title="Pokémon Omega Ruby and Alpha Sapphire">Pokémon Omega Ruby and Alpha Sapphire</a>, Secret Pals at the player's <a href="/wiki/Secret_Base" title="Secret Base">Secret Base</a> can decrease an Egg's current Egg cycle count by half of its base Egg cycle count, rounded up.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Generations_III_and_IV">Generations III and IV</span></h2>
<p>Every time an Egg cycle is completed, the game goes through the Eggs in the player's party in order and performs the following:
</p>
<ul><li> If the Egg's Egg cycle count is 0, the Egg hatches and no other Eggs are processed.</li>
<li> Otherwise, subtract 1 from the Egg's cycle count.
<ul><li> In <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Emerald_Version" title="Pokémon Emerald Version">Pokémon Emerald</a> or Generation IV games, if a Pokémon with <a href="/wiki/Flame_Body_(Ability)" title="Flame Body (Ability)">Flame Body</a> or <a href="/wiki/Magma_Armor_(Ability)" title="Magma Armor (Ability)">Magma Armor</a> is in the party, subtract 2 instead of 1 (but to no less than 0).</li></ul></li></ul>
<p>As a consequence of this logic, in order to hatch a given Egg, the player must walk one more Egg cycle than the Egg's base Egg cycle value. As an example, a new <a href="/wiki/Magikarp_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Magikarp (Pokémon)">Magikarp</a> Egg has an Egg cycle value of 5, but the player must walk 6 Egg cycles in order to hatch it. By the same token, if a Pokémon with <a href="/wiki/Flame_Body_(Ability)" title="Flame Body (Ability)">Flame Body</a> or <a href="/wiki/Magma_Armor_(Ability)" title="Magma Armor (Ability)">Magma Armor</a> is in the party, instead of an Egg taking <code>base_Egg_cycles / 2</code> (rounded up) Egg cycles to hatch, <code>base_Egg_cycles / 2 + 1</code> (rounded up) Egg cycles must be walked.
</p><p>When an Egg is received from the Day Care Man, the counter for the current number of steps taken in the current Egg cycle is set to 1 in Generation III or to 0 in Generation IV.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Generation_II">Generation II</span></h2>
<p>Every time an Egg cycle is completed, the game goes through the Eggs in the player's party in order and performs the following:
</p>
<ul><li> Subtract 1 from the Egg's cycle count. If its Egg cycle count is now 0, the Egg hatches and no other Eggs are processed.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Quotes">Quotes</span></h2>
<p>The quote shown from the table below depends solely on the Egg cycle value in the Egg's Pokémon data structure. That is, since, in Generations III and IV, the number of Egg cycles remaining for the player to walk before an Egg hatches is one greater than the value in the Egg's data structure, the maximum number of Egg cycles the player must walk is not the maximum shown in the leftmost cell, but one greater than that value. As an example, in <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Diamond_and_Pearl_Versions" title="Pokémon Diamond and Pearl Versions">Pokémon Diamond and Pearl</a>, a new <a href="/wiki/Magikarp_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Magikarp (Pokémon)">Magikarp</a> Egg has a base 5 Egg cycles and will show the quote <i>"Sounds can be heard coming from inside! It will hatch soon!"</i> on its summary screen, but the player will have to walk 6 Egg cycles before the Egg will hatch.
</p>
